
> Web-Crawler-Nodejs@1.0.0 statistics C:\Users\denev\Documents\Code\Web-Crawler-Nodejs
> node ./statistics/statistics.js "order-by" "vendor"

Executing (default): SELECT `model`.`id`, `vendor`.`name`, `model`.`name` AS `model`, `model`.`price`, `model`.`picture`, `specs`.`type`, `specs`.`value`, `stores`.`name`, `vendor`.`id` AS `vendor.id`, `vendor`.`name` AS `vendor.name`, `stores`.`id` AS `stores.id`, `stores`.`name` AS `stores.name`, `stores->model_store`.`createdAt` AS `stores.model_store.createdAt`, `stores->model_store`.`updatedAt` AS `stores.model_store.updatedAt`, `stores->model_store`.`modelId` AS `stores.model_store.modelId`, `stores->model_store`.`storeId` AS `stores.model_store.storeId`, `specs`.`id` AS `specs.id`, `specs`.`type` AS `specs.type`, `specs`.`value` AS `specs.value`, `specs->model_specs`.`createdAt` AS `specs.model_specs.createdAt`, `specs->model_specs`.`updatedAt` AS `specs.model_specs.updatedAt`, `specs->model_specs`.`modelId` AS `specs.model_specs.modelId`, `specs->model_specs`.`specId` AS `specs.model_specs.specId` FROM `models` AS `model` LEFT OUTER JOIN `vendors` AS `vendor` ON `model`.`vendorId` = `vendor`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN ( `model_store` AS `stores->model_store` INNER JOIN `stores` AS `stores` ON `stores`.`id` = `stores->model_store`.`storeId`) ON `model`.`id` = `stores->model_store`.`modelId` LEFT OUTER JOIN ( `model_specs` AS `specs->model_specs` INNER JOIN `specs` AS `specs` ON `specs`.`id` = `specs->model_specs`.`specId`) ON `model`.`id` = `specs->model_specs`.`modelId` ORDER BY `vendor`.`name`;
